x:leading-7","children":[["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"@agentica"}]," is specialized in LLM (Large Language Model) function calling, and doing everything with the function calling. Complex agent workflows and graphs required in conventional AI agent development are not necessary in ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"@agentica"}],". Only LLM function calling schema is important, and ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"@agentica"}]," will do everything with it. Therefore, the most important thing in ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"@agentica"}]," based development is, how safely and efficiently build the LLM function calling schema."]}],"\n",["$","p",null,{"className":"x:not-first:mt-6 x:leading-7","children":["By the way, what if a person writes a function calling schema by hand and makes a mistake? It will break the entire AI agent system, because the LLM function calling would never be successful with the wrong schema. For example, in the case of a traditional backend development, if a backend developer takes a mistake in the API documentation, the frontend developer (human) can intuitively avoid it. However, ",["$","strong",null,{"children":"AI never forgives"}]," such mistakes."]}],"\n",["$","p",null,{"className":"x:not-first:mt-6 x:leading-7","children":"To prevent such human mistakes, the LLM function calling schema must be constructed by the compiler. I call this concept as “Compiler Driven Development”."}],"\n",["$","h3",null,{"id":"typescript-class","className":"x:tracking-tight x:text-slate-900 x:dark:text-slate-100 x:font-semibold x:target:animate-[fade-in_1.5s] x:mt-8 x:text-2xl","children":["TypeScript Class",["$","$L1e",null,{"id":"typescript-class"}]]}],"\n",["$","p",null,{"className":"x:not-first:mt-6 x:leading-7","children":["Use ",["$","a",null,{"href":"https://typia.io/docs/llm/application","target":"_blank","rel":"noreferrer","className":"x:focus-visible:nextra-focus x:text-primary-600 x:underline x:hover:no-underline x:decoration-from-font x:[text-underline-position:from-font]","children":[["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"typia.llm.application<Class, Model>()"}],false]}]," function."]}],"\n",["$","p",null,{"className":"x:not-first:mt-6 x:leading-7","children":[["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"@agentica"}]," is guiding to use ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"typia.llm.application<Class, Model>()"}]," function when constructing a function calling schema for a TypeScript class method. And ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"typia"}]," is the only one library which can create LLM function calling schema from the TypeScript class type.
